 Now thank United Payments Interface (UPI) that the process of mobile payment has reached a new stage
 yah apane kism kii duniya main iklauti aplication he
 People of India are now addicted to paying with cards etc
 upiai ne isamen ek kadam or aage badhaayaa he jiske tahat aapako apane smartphone par paise praapt karne vaale kii virtual aaidi ko daalana hota he or uske baad ap ek pin maangata he jise phir se daalana hota he
 After this, the money automatically goes from your account to the recipient's account and it only takes a few minutes
 iske liye na aapako apana bank khaataa vivaran dena hoga or na hi praptakarta ke bank kaa iefessi code
 You can transact millions in a few easy steps
 jaruri nahin ki aapke phone main ap usee bank kaa ho jisamen aapkaa khaataa he, balki kisi bhi anya bank kaa ho saktaa he jo aapako behatar anubhav detaa ho
 The same applies with the recipient
 paison kaa len-dein haalanki aapke or praptakarta ke bainkon ke bich hi hota he or aapako iskaa pataa tak nahin lagata
 Now, with the worry of carrying cash or stealing credit card details, freedom is about to come
 is kaam ko neshnal pements korporation of india (enpisiai) anjaam de rahaa he, jo bharat main sabhi khudara bhugtanon ke maamle ko dekhne vaala sanghathan he jo bhartiya rigerv bank ke maatahat kaam karata he
 It has ten promoter banks: State Bank of India, Punjab National Bank, Canara Bank, Bank of Baroda, Union Bank of India, Bank of India, ICICI Bank, HDFC Bank, Citibank and HSBC
 is ap ko viksit karne main 15 logon kii ek team kaam kar rahi he or vibhinn bainkon kii takneekee tiimon ke saath samanvay main he taaki ise saakaar kiya ja sake
 Is this a new app? UPI will not have an app of its own, rather it will allow banks to add the function of UPI to their existing app, or banks will be able to create their own separate UPI app

 Paytm will be different from UPI? An important difference between an app like Paytm and UPI will be that Paytm is a half-incomplete mobile wallet
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki jo koi petm main panjikrut he, vahi usase len-dein kar saktaa he
